    SELECT TOP(1) [e].[Id], [e].[ActionType], [e].[Code], [e].[CreatedDate], [e].[Definition], [e].[HttpType], [e].[MenuId], [e].[Name], [e].[Status], [e].[UpdatedDate]
    FROM [Endpoints] AS [e]
    WHERE [e].[Code] = @__code_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[ActionsId], [a].[RolesId], [a0].[Id], [a0].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a0].[CreatedDate], [a0].[IsActive], [a0].[Name], [a0].[NormalizedName]
    FROM [AppRoleEndpoint] AS [a]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetRoles] AS [a0] ON [a].[RolesId] = [a0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ActionsId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t0].[ActionsId], [t0].[RolesId], [t0].[Id]
